msg:We recently had the pleasure of spending a wonderful time at Shuangman Fuyuan International Hotel, and I have to say that the services and facilities provided by this hotel exceeded all my expectations:

Excellent location: Located in a prime location in the city center, it is very convenient for exploring Ordos' cultural attractions, shopping areas and food streets. The hotel is well-connected to transportation and parking, and you can easily reach any place you want to go.

Room comfort: The room is elegantly decorated and the bed is comfortable, which makes people have a perfect sleeping experience. The space is spacious and the facilities are complete. Every detail reflects the hotel's thoughtful consideration of guests' needs.

Service quality: The professionalism and friendliness of the staff are impressive. From the front desk to the room service, everyone shows extremely high service standards and hospitality. They are helpful and can respond quickly and provide solutions to any problems.

Dining experience: The breakfast ingredients in the hotel are fresh, delicious, and varied, especially the milk tea with milk skin is delicious. The front desk reception also gave us a breakfast and a plate of fruit. Whether it is local specialties or other delicacies, you can find them here.

Cleanliness and safety: The hotel's cleanliness standards are very high, and both public and private areas are kept extremely clean and tidy. In addition, the hotel's security measures also make me feel at ease, ensuring the privacy and safety of guests.

Shuangman Fuyuan International Hotel is a hotel that provides excellent service, comfortable accommodation and first-class facilities. We are very satisfied with this stay. Whether it is a business trip or a leisure vacation, I will not hesitate to choose this place again and warmly recommend it to my friends.

msg:Located in Kangbashi District of Ordos City, there are relatively few people. The hotel has a very Mongolian style of decoration and a blue and white yurt color scheme.
Complaint point 1: This is also the most unsatisfactory point. I live on the 21st floor, and there is no hot water in the room of more than 700 yuan. Can you believe that there is no hot water in the quasi-five-star room? The hotel told me that it was because the floor was too high. The solution was to go to the 10th floor early in the morning to open a room for me to take a shower;
Complaint point 2: It can also be accepted when booking a room. It shows that there are welcome fruits, but there are none. We booked two rooms together and there was no hot water and fruit;
Advantages: The breakfast is really very good, very rich and there are many kinds. It is a Mongolian breakfast. Here I emphasize that there are three kinds of noodles: buckwheat, mixed noodles, and white noodles; there are also three kinds of sauerkraut: lamb, pork, tomato and egg.
I sincerely hope that the hotel can improve its level of occupancy.
